</pre>
## Idea

A type is `π_n`-finite if it has finitely many connected components and all of its homotopy groups up to level `n` at all base points are finite.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="6778" class="Comment">-- Section 1. π-Finiteness</a>

<a id="6806" class="Comment">-- Definition 1.3</a>

<a id="6825" class="Comment">-- We introduce locally finite types</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-Prop"></a><a id="6863" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#6863" class="Function">is-locally-finite-Prop</a> <a id="6886" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="8675" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#5874" class="Function">prod-Prop</a> <a id="8685" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8687" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8516" class="Function">is-π-finite-Prop</a> <a id="8704" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1551" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕ</a> <a id="8711" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8669" class="Bound">X</a><a id="8712" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="8726" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8728" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#6694" class="Function">Π-Prop</a> <a id="8735" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8669" class="Bound">X</a>
              <a id="8751" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8753" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="8755" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8755" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8757" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8759" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#6694" class="Function">Π-Prop</a> <a id="8766" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8669" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="8768" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8771" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8771" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8773" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8775" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8516" class="Function">is-π-finite-Prop</a> <a id="8792" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8666" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="8794" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8795" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1767" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="8798" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8755" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8800" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#8771" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8801" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="9375" class="Comment">-- Basic properties of locally finite types</a>

<a id="9420" class="Comment">-- locally finite types are closed under equivalences</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-equiv"></a><a id="9475" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9475" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9499" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9503" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9504" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9504" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="9507" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9507" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="9510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9512" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9517" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9519" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9520" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9520" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9522" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9524" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9527" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9504" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="9529" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9531" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9532" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9532" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9534" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9536" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9539" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9507" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="9541" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9544" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9544" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9546" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9548" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9520" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9550" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="9552" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9532" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9553" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9555" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9559" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#7009" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9577" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9532" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9579" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9581" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#7009" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9599" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9520" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="9601" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9475" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9625" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9625" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9627" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9627" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9629" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9629" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9631" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9631" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9633" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="9637" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#7295" class="Function">is-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9654" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9655" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#16746" class="Function">equiv-ap</a> <a id="9664" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9625" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9666" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9629" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9668" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9631" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9669" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9672" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9627" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="9674" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9675" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="9685" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9625" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9687" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9629" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9688" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9691" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="9701" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9625" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9703" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9631" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9704" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;"></a><a id="9708" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9708" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9733" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9737" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9738" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9738" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="9741" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9741" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="9744" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9746" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9751" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9753" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9754" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9754" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9756" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9758" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9761" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9738" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="9763" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9765" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9766" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9766" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9768" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9770" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="9773" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9741" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="9775" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9777" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9778" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9778" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9780" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9782" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9754" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9784" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="9786" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9766" class="Bound">B</a><a id="9787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9789" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9793" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#7009" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9811" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9754" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9813" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9815" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#7009" class="Function">is-locally-finite</a> <a id="9833" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9766" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="9835" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9708" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv&#39;</a> <a id="9860" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9860" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="9862" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9864" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9475" class="Function">is-locally-finite-equiv</a> <a id="9888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9889" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5721" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="9899" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9860" class="Bound">e</a><a id="9900" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="9903" class="Comment">-- types with decidable equality are locally finite</a>

<a id="is-locally-finite-has-decidable-equality"></a><a id="9956" href="univalent-combinatorics.pi-finite-types.html#9956" class="Function">is-locally-finite-has-decidable-equality</a> <a id="9997" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="18812" class="Comment">-- Dependent product of locally finite types</a>
